 rajyasabha main sheetakaaleen satr main vidheyak par hui bahes ke dauraan sadasyon ne 149 sanshodhan prastaav pesh kiye the
 The source said that talks are being held with the leaders of various parties and efforts are on to reach an agreement on key issues
 tippaniyan The official said that Lokayukta Bill 2011 has made provision for Lokayukta as there is no uniformity in the Lokayukta Act which exists in different states
 pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne 23 march is masale par sahmati banane ke liye sarvadaleey baithak bulaai thi lekin adhiktar netaaon ne lokapal vidheyak se lokayukta ko alag kiye jane ke paksh main apane vichaar rakhe the
 The source said that the Lokpal amended bill is currently in the Rajya Sabha
 yahaan se paarit hone ke baad ise phir se loksabhaa se paarit karana hoga jo ki bajet satr main sambhav najar nahin aata
 The official source said that currently Minister of State in the Prime Minister's Office V
 narayansami anaupchaarik taur par vibhinn dalon ke netaaon se baatcheet kar rahe hai ki vidheyak ko kis tarah aage badhaayaa jaae
 During the debate on the bill in the Rajya Sabha in the winter session, 149 amendment proposals were moved by the members
 sutara ne kaha ki vibhinn dalon ke netaaon se baatcheet kii ja rahi he or pramukh muddon par sahmati banane kaa prayaas jari he
 The comments adhikari ne kaha ki lokapal vidheyak 2011 main lokayukta kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he kyonki vibhinn rajyon main maujuud lokayukta kanoon main samanta nahin he
 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh had called an all-party meeting on March 23 to agree on this issue, but most of the leaders had expressed their views in favor of the separation of Lokayukta from the Lokpal Bill
